Page 11

Local News Two

Detailed Report on the Zhenru Train Collision 147

More than 30 Passengers Injured

Lu Zhichuan's Wife Most Severely Injured

All Trains Have Resumed Normal Operation

Those Responsible for the Accident Suspended Pending Investigation

The previous report briefly described the collision between the 207th freight train and the 10th passenger train on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway at Zhenru Station. It is now known that the cause of the collision was very complicated. The details are described as follows:

Cause of the Train Collision 148

At 9:46 PM last night, the 202nd down freight train from Nanjing to Shanghai was stopped on the straight track at Zhenru Station. Because the Meigen Road Station was preparing to dispatch the 207th up freight train and had already obtained the road sign from Zhenru Station, Zhenru Station detained the 202nd freight train to wait for the 207th train. After the 207th freight train arrived at Zhenru Station at 10:03 and stopped properly on the bay track, the 202nd freight train was released from Zhenru to Meigen Road. However, the 10th express train and the 4th passenger train from Nanjing to Shanghai had also departed from Nanxiang and Anting stations. The 207th freight train had no chance to be released. The stationmaster detained the freight train and prepared to release it after meeting the two passenger trains. Unexpectedly, Wu Shengorong, the switchman of the western branch track of the station, saw that the 207th train had met the 202nd train at the station and assumed that the 207th train should be released to Nanxiang. He did not wait for the stationmaster's hand signal and immediately switched the track to the bay track for the 202nd train to pass through. At that time, the stationmaster was the substitute stationmaster Yang Wenyi, who was teaching the tenth train road sign to Nanxiang Station in the office and reporting the train schedule. When the signal from Nanxiang Station that the tenth train had left Nanxiang Station was received, he routinely instructed the porter Lian Asan to turn down the signal flag to let the train enter the station. However, the switchman Wu Shengorong in the switch shed did not pay attention to the signal flag being turned down, and that the track he had switched was for the bay track. When the stationmaster discovered that the track was switched incorrectly, he quickly blew the whistle and signaled to switch it to the straight track. But at that time, the tenth train had already entered the Zhenru Station outside the signal flag and was about to reach the signal flag switch. Although the switchman discovered it, it was too late. Therefore, the tenth train entered the bay track, and at the same time, the 207th freight train, which had stopped on the bay track, had no headlights. Therefore, the driver of the tenth train did not pay attention. When the train approached, he immediately braked, but the momentum was too great to stop immediately, and this unfortunate accident occurred at 10:30.

Train Cars Overturned 149

When the two trains collided, the sound shook the fields. Fortunately, the 207th freight train was not moving, which was already a great fortune. Otherwise, the consequences would have been unimaginable. When the 207th train was hit, the rear part of the B-38 locomotive immediately fell into the track. The two coal cars behind the locomotive immediately jumped out, overturned, and fell into the straight track. On the tenth train, only the C-13 locomotive was completely trapped in the track. All the window glass of the second-class car behind the locomotive was shattered by the severe shock, and many of the seats and tables in the car collapsed. The light luggage on the car frame also fell down, making the car extremely messy. A total of eight rails and more than forty sleepers were destroyed.

Passengers Injured 150

Yesterday, the tenth train was on time. Most passengers were organizing their belongings as they approached Shanghai. When the two trains collided, the momentum was too strong, and they all fainted and fell due to the shock. Some were injured by tables and chairs, some were injured by mutual collisions, some were injured by glass, and some were injured by falling objects. A total of about 30 people were injured. The car was covered in bloodstains, and groans were endless. Among them, the wife of Lu Zhichuan, who was coming to Shanghai from Suzhou, was the most seriously injured in the abdomen. Five waiters and one cook in the kitchen of the car, and a passenger named Cai Meizhang who boarded the train in Wanlin, were all injured in the head. The waiter Feng Jujin and the passenger Yan Dehou were both injured in the legs. The train conductor of the tenth train, Fei Bangyan, suffered a scalp abrasion. More than 20 other passengers suffered minor injuries to their hands and feet, or waist and chest pain. There was also a soldier who was seriously injured in the chest.

Great Rescue 151

The accident site was near Jinan University. When the Boy Scouts of the school heard the news, they rushed to the scene of the accident to check. Seeing that the passengers were injured and the railway medical officer had not yet arrived, they quickly returned to the school, brought medicine, bandaged the injured passengers in the car, and maintained order. The spirit of chivalry was admirable.

Railway Bureau Rescue 152

After the accident, the Railway Bureau immediately dispatched senior officials from the Traffic Department to find a way to drag out the rescue car and notify the railway doctor and all the craftsmen. They departed together on the rescue car at 1:40 AM yesterday morning. A single locomotive was dispatched to Zhenru in advance to drag the vehicles of the 207th freight train that were not affected back to Meigen Road. The rescue car arrived at Zhenru at 1:55 AM. The officials immediately divided the work. First, they rescued the injured and sent them to various hospitals. Those who did not want to go to the hospital were sent to the North Station. Then, they quickly lifted the two coal cars that had fallen into the straight track and cleared the coal to clear the straight track. At 3:20 AM yesterday morning, the straight track was cleared. The tenth train was withdrawn from the bay track and advanced to the straight track. Another locomotive was dispatched to drag it back to the North Station at 3:40 AM.

Traffic Situation 153

After the accident, obstacles occurred on the way, so the trains could not travel to and fro. The night train from Nanjing to Beijing at 11:45 PM was delayed until 4:53 AM yesterday morning to leave the North Station, a delay of five hours. The night train from Beijing to Shanghai arrived at port at about 8:00 AM yesterday morning. The fourth special express train from Beijing to Shanghai at 4:00 PM the day before was delayed until 4:20 AM yesterday morning to arrive at the North Station. Now, the bay track at Zhenru Station has been severely damaged and cannot be repaired immediately. However, the straight track can still be used normally. Therefore, all trains have returned to normal yesterday.

Aftermath 154

According to yesterday's news, the station master's side was indeed at fault in this incident, but the track switchman's unauthorized handling of train schedules, disregarding signals, was the biggest cause of the accident. At the same time, the No. 207 freight train's locomotive did not have a headlight, making it impossible to distinguish, which was also inappropriate. Otherwise, the collision would not have been so severe. Currently, all involved parties in the case have been temporarily suspended from their positions by the Railway Bureau and are awaiting interrogation in Shanghai. Once the truth is revealed, further action will be taken.

American Attitude Towards the Noulens Case 155

Dewey and Others Jointly Protest

Request Madam Soong Ching-ling to Find a Way to Rescue

After the news of the Noulens couple, previously believed to be representatives of the Pan-Pacific Trade Union headquarters and members of the Communist Party, being sentenced to death in Nanjing, reached the United States via telegram, prominent Americans were greatly shocked. These prominent figures, who are usually engaged in the protection of people's private and public rights, sent a joint telegram to the Nanjing National Government and another telegram to Madam Soong Ching-ling on October 24, protesting the shocking verdict. The signatories included Clarence Darrow, Theodore Dreiser, Louis Gannett, Norman Thomas, Louis Untermeyer, John Dewey, and others. Darrow is a famous Chicago lawyer and a free thinker who often uses the American spirit of freedom enshrined in the American Declaration of Independence as his fundamental concept. In the past twenty-five years, he has been known in the United States as a protector of workers and political prisoners. In famous American trials of workers, he was almost always the leading defense lawyer, and was thus honored with the title of "Protector of Labor." Dreiser is one of America's two great writers, author of many novels. Europeans mostly regard him as America's greatest literary figure. He is the author of *Genius*, *Sister Carrie*, and many short stories. His recent book, *An American Tragedy*, is currently being shown on Shanghai screens. Gannett is also a free thinker who traveled extensively to major cities in China five years ago and is the editor of the famous New York-based *The Nation*. He currently writes for the *New York Herald Tribune*. Baldwin is the secretary-general of the American Civil Liberties Union, a national organization whose mission is to protect the freedom of speech, publication, assembly, and the right to strike for all people through newspapers and lawyers. Baldwin is a pacifist and also a free thinker. Dewey is a famous educator and philosopher, currently a professor at Columbia University. His theories are well known in universities in China that have educational programs, so there is no need for a detailed introduction.

Husband Returns to Clan, Wife Disagrees 156

Lu Zhongen Has Returned to the Hua Clan

His Wife Sues to Establish Her Status

Does the Wife's Status Depend on Her Husband's?

Court Scheduled to Pronounce Judgment on the 31st

Lu Dongsen, a native of Dinghai residing at 227 Yanqing Lane, Xiamen Road, was old-fashioned, so he ordered his son Zhongen, who had also come of age and was working for the Municipal Council, to marry Kang Xindi as his wife. They officially married last year and now have a son. Unexpectedly, Lu Dongsen and his son suddenly had a falling out this spring and became involved in a lawsuit. Lu claimed that Zhongen was not his biological son and requested permission to sever their father-son relationship. After the first instance judgment, one party was dissatisfied and appealed. The second division of the Jiangsu High Court summoned both parties to court for questioning. As a result, Lu Dongsen was granted permission to sever his father-son relationship with Lu Zhongen, and Lu Dongsen was ordered to pay Lu Zhongen 800 yuan within three months. Since then, Zhongen has reverted to his original Hua surname. However, Zhongen's wife, Kang Xindi, claimed that since her husband had returned to his clan, she had not agreed to it beforehand. Therefore, she filed a lawsuit against her father-in-law, Lu Dongsen, to establish her status and requested that the defendant, Lu Dongsen, return the gifted property he was holding in trust. According to Kang's complaint, in 1923, when she was fifteen years old, her parents betrothed her to Zhongen, the son of the defendant Lu Dongsen. In April 1925, after the death of her aunt-in-law, Lu Zhao, the defendant followed the customs of his hometown and welcomed her into the family to observe mourning and filial piety. He also gave her a portion of her aunt's belongings as a gift. At that time, she was still young and had no ability to manage them, so she handed them over to the defendant to hold in trust. In 1930, she officially married the defendant's son, Lu Zhongen, and soon gave birth to a son named Lu Painan, who is not yet one year old. In the spring of this year, the defendant and his son suddenly became involved in a lawsuit. The defendant claimed that Zhongen was the son of Hua Shen and was adopted by the defendant when he was young. In the second instance, they reached a settlement. Zhongen admitted to severing his father-son relationship with the defendant and returning to the Hua surname. However, she was not consulted about the case beforehand or afterward, and the settlement resulted in her and her son Painan changing their surnames and leaving the Lu family to become members of the Hua family. She believes that her previously acquired name rights and Lu family status should be protected by Article 083 of the Civil Code. She has requested mediation, but the defendant refused. Therefore, she has filed a lawsuit requesting a judgment: (1) Confirming Lu Kang Xindi's status as Lu Dongsen's daughter-in-law; (2) Confirming Lu Painan as Lu Dongsen's grandson; (3) Lu Dongsen should return the entrusted items according to the list; (4) The defendant should bear the costs of this lawsuit. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang opened the court to examine the case. In addition to the two parties, Hua Zhongen (i.e., Lu Zhongen) was also summoned to testify. First, the plaintiff stated the reasons for the lawsuit. Then, the defendant provided rebuttal, stating that it was because Zhongen's character was too poor and he had no respect for his elders that they severed their father-son relationship. As for the surname of the daughter-in-law, it should naturally follow her husband. Moreover, her son was born in her mother's home, so he cannot be recognized as a grandson. He also denied the other requests of the plaintiff. Later, the plaintiff's lawyer, Li Shiwei, and the defendant's lawyer, Liu, debated each other based on the law. Lawyer Li argued that although the law does not stipulate that the consent of the spouse is required for an adopted son to return to his clan, if it hinders the rights of a third party, then it is necessary to request legal protection. Moreover, what was severed was the relationship of an adopted son, not an adopted daughter-in-law or adopted grandson, so the status of the plaintiff and her son should be confirmed. The plaintiff is a weak woman, and Painan is still in swaddling clothes. Their future life cannot be supported by Zhongen and must rely on the defendant. Lawyer Liu argued that the wife should follow her husband. After both sides finished their arguments, Judge Yang adjourned the court and scheduled the judgment for the 31st of this month.

Mercury Mixed in Noodles 157

Wu Yantian Accuses Wife of Attempted Murder

Bian Shi Firmly Denies

Wu Yantian, a coppersmith from Nanjing residing at 316 Ruijin Road, has been constantly arguing with his wife, Bian Shi (age 31), due to financial difficulties. Around 10 AM yesterday morning, Wu Yantian planned to marry off his eleven-year-old daughter to a certain family as a child bride. Bian Shi did not agree, and another argument ensued. After a while, Bian Shi went out to buy 200 *wen* worth of fresh noodles and brought them home to cook for lunch, adding a little bit of vegetables. After they were cooked, they were divided into three bowls, and the couple and their daughter ate them one after another. Wu felt that the noodles tasted strange while he was eating. After he finished eating, noodle soup suddenly flowed out of his mouth and dripped on the table. Upon inspection, it was mercury. He carefully looked at the remaining juice at the bottom of the bowl and found traces of the substance. He then questioned Bian Shi, "Did you put this poisonous substance in here to try to murder me?" Bian Shi denied it, and another argument ensued. Wu immediately reported the incident to the Harbin Police Station, which dispatched Chinese detective Peng Yushan and Western detective McLaren to take Bian Shi and the noodle bowl to the police station, where she was transferred to the women's prison. At the same time, Wu Yantian was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment. Yesterday morning, the police station escorted Wu Bian Shi to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District. The police station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, presented the case and stated that the victim, Wu Yantian, was fortunate to have only been slightly poisoned. After treatment by doctors, his life was not in danger. He was present in court to be questioned. Chinese detective Peng Yushan reported that after the incident, he had investigated the noodle shop that Bian Shi had mentioned, and there was no mercury mixed in. He then presented the large bowl Wu had used to eat the noodles at the time for inspection. The victim, Wu Yantian, stated that he used to be a patrol officer and now worked as a coppersmith. He has been married to Bian Shi for eleven years and has two daughters. The couple's relationship was good in the past, but recently, due to a declining livelihood and financial difficulties, Bian Shi often argued with him. He had mentioned the matter of marrying off his eleven-year-old daughter as a child bride to someone several times before, but it had not yet been carried out. He then described the events in detail. When questioned, Wu Bian Shi stated that she had been married to Wu for eleven years and that he often quarreled with her. Yesterday morning, he wanted to marry off their eleven-year-old daughter to someone as a child bride. She did not agree, and another argument ensued. He said, "If you like someone, you can follow them immediately, but you have to give me money." As for the mercury in the noodles, it was actually a false accusation by him. If she wanted to murder him, she would have done it long ago. Why wait eleven years? She asked for a fair judgment. After examining the statements, Judge Xiao Xiefen ordered Wu Bian Shi to be detained for further investigation and interrogation.

New Regulations on the Elimination of Obstructions on Sidewalks 163

Promulgated by the Municipal Council

In view of the increasing number of sidewalks obstructed by permanent or movable objects, the Municipal Council has now decided that the following regulations must be strictly observed in the future. In the past, there have been many violators who were ordered by the Municipal Council to remove wooden signs placed on the sidewalk or to raise tents that were hanging low over the sidewalk, but the obstructions were soon returned to their original locations. Therefore, general measures are hereby formulated to eliminate such obstructions. However, in order to allow shop owners and others sufficient time to comply with the new regulations, these measures will be implemented from January 1, 1932. At that time, the Municipal Council will exercise the powers conferred by Clause 23 of the Land Regulations to implement the following new regulations: (1) Tents or parts thereof shall not be installed at a height of less than seven feet six inches above the sidewalk or at a height of less than fifteen feet above the road surface; (2) No fixtures, stalls, stands or other movable objects shall be placed in front of any building in such a way as to protrude onto the sidewalk or roadway.

Clause 23 of the Land Regulations provides that if any porch, veranda, awning, casement, steps, cellar, cellar door or window, wooden or iron sign, shelf, shutter, wall, fence or any other projecting object, whether constructed or placed, protrudes from any building or in front of any building within the boundary and is sufficient to obstruct the safety and passage of the road, the Council may notify the occupant of the building to remove or reconstruct the obstruction. The occupant shall remove or reconstruct the object in accordance with the Council's instructions within fourteen days of receipt of the notice. If the occupant fails to do so, the Council may impose a fine of up to ten dollars and remove the obstruction on his behalf. The cost of removal shall be borne by the occupant and may be recovered by way of damages. However, if the obstruction was created or installed by the owner, the cost of removal paid by the occupant may be deducted from the rent.

Lawsuit Regarding the Biography of Wu King Zhang Shicheng 164

Han Zishi Wrote a Book About a Local Sage

Zhao Nangong Breached the Contract and Did Not Publish It

Zhang Shicheng, the Wu King at the end of the Yuan Dynasty, was originally from Taixian, Jiangsu Province. When Zhang ruled the three Wu regions, he was known for his political achievements and left a legacy of love among the people. Han Zishi, a former Jiangsu Province official, regarded Zhang as an elder from his hometown. He collected local literature and wrote a biography, which he completed last June. Through the introduction of Zhao Yuansheng, an employee of the Nanshi Electric Company in this city, Han handed over the manuscript to Zhao Nangong, the manager of the Taidong Bookstore on the Fourth Avenue, to negotiate the printing. They agreed on the cost of labor and materials and signed a contract, setting a deadline for delivery. However, Zhao repeatedly delayed the delivery. Therefore, Han entrusted lawyers Zhu Shaowen and Zhu Dianqing to file a petition with the mediation office of the First Special District Court for mediation. The petition is recorded as follows: "For breach of contract and damages, requesting mediation to order performance within a time limit or termination of the contract and return of funds. The petitioner, on June 18 of last year, through the introduction of Zhao Yuansheng, handed over the Wu King Zhang Shicheng biography written by the petitioner to the Taidong Bookstore managed by the opposing party for printing. The opposing party issued a quotation list, totaling 1,685 yuan. It was agreed that the petitioner would pay 40% and the opposing party would pay 60%, and each would receive 500 copies of the book. It was agreed that the book would be completed within one month. The petitioner paid the 40%, totaling 674 yuan, in full. Unexpectedly, a lawsuit suddenly occurred at the printing press of the bookstore. The paper plates that had been made were taken away. The petitioner repeatedly urged the opposing party, who first said that they were investigating, and then said that they had been taken away by the landlord. After urging for half a year, the book was still not printed. The petitioner had no choice but to request your court to summon the opposing party to mediate, ordering them to perform the contract within a time limit, or terminate the contract, compensate for the deposit and manuscript, and clear the formalities. We look forward to this very much." This case will be summoned for mediation between the two parties soon.

A Young Man in a Suit Commits Fraudulent Acts 165

Deceives Wang Kunli to Obtain Medicine

Deceives Chen Xishan to Obtain Telegram

Deceives Wang's Mother to Give 30 Yuan

Discovered and Escapes, Then Captured

Chen Xishan, a 36-year-old Henan native, resides at 29 Xianxian Lane, Hujun Camp, Nanshi. Chen has a cousin, Wang Kunli, who resides at Chen's place. The woman is currently 29 years old. Her father, Wang Xiqing, works as a locomotive mechanic at the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Station. Yesterday morning, he went to Hangzhou by train. Around 2 PM, a young man wearing a fancy suit suddenly visited Chen's home to see Wang Kunli. Chen happened to be sleeping upstairs, so Wang came out to greet him. The young man said that her father, Wang Xiqing, had gone to Hangzhou on official business this morning and was hit by a train in Jiaxing, injuring his waist severely and potentially endangering his life. Wang was shocked to hear this, as if struck by lightning. The young man continued, "Now, you don't need to panic. You should quickly go to my friend Zhao Jintian's house at 39 Fuhe Lane near the Great World in the northern part of the city and ask Zhao for a bottle of wound medicine. Because this medicine has miraculous effects when applied to wounds. After you get the medicine, quickly come back and take the 3 o'clock express train with me to Jiaxing to accompany your father back to Shanghai." Wang, anxious about her father, did not bother to think carefully and immediately went to Fuhe Lane near the Great World to get the wound medicine. On the way, she suddenly remembered that the young man had said that her father was seriously injured and in danger, and that the medicine would probably be ineffective. It would be better to go to the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Station to inquire about the situation. After Wang left home, Chen Xishan heard the noise and woke up. After going downstairs and talking to the young man, he was also greatly shocked. The young man also said that there was a telegram from Wang Xiqing at the North Railway Station, asking him to retrieve it. Chen observed the young man's actions and found them to be suspicious. He immediately went out to inquire about the facts at the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Station first. Seeing Chen go out, the young man said to Wang's mother, "Later, I will go to Jiaxing with your daughter to pick up Mr. Wang Xiqing and bring him home. But we are short of travel expenses. Please give me 30 yuan for expenses." Wang's mother was old and weak, and she did not think carefully at the time, so she paid the full amount. The young man, having obtained the money, was about to leave when Wang and Chen returned home after inquiring about the news at the station. Since there was no such thing, they knew something was wrong. They rushed home and asked Wang's mother about the payment, only to realize that they had been deceived. Seeing Chen and the others return, the young man knew that the matter had been exposed. His face turned pale instantly. He ran out the door and fled. Chen immediately chased after him, shouting "Catch him! Catch him!" Hearing this, the guard Yuan Huairen from the 26th post and the police officer Ma Huaiyi from the 24th post rushed over and intercepted the young man. They searched him on the spot and found the original 30 yuan. They took him to the First Precinct of the First District. During the preliminary interrogation by the director of the precinct, Wang Kunli and Chen Xishan complained about the previous events and requested a thorough investigation. When questioned, the young man stated that his name was Wang Yonghai, 21 years old, from Shandong. My father, Wang Guanzhi, is currently the station master at Jiaxing Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway. My cousin, Liu Chao, is currently the captain of the Fifth Aviation Team of the National Revolutionary Army in Nanjing. I was studying at the Japanese Military Academy. When the Japanese invaded the Northeast, we returned to China by boat. I am currently staying at the YMCA near the Great World. My cousin Liu Chao has a friend, Chen, who is a high-ranking official at the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Station. Today, he called and said that Wang Xiqing was injured by a train at Jiaxing Station, so he told me to notify his family and ask them to go to Jiaxing to bring Wang back to Shanghai for treatment." The rest of his words were evasive. As the matter involved fraud, he was ordered to be detained for verification.

Russian Man Shoots Himself 166

Quarreled with Wife and Took His Own Life in Anger

Ziling, a 26-year-old Russian, works at the Machine Manufacturing Factory at 695 Avenue Joffre in the French Concession and also serves in the Shanghai Volunteer Corps in the International Settlement. With a loud bang, the bullet entered from his forehead and pierced through the back of his head. Zhang Yinan, a native of Nanxiang who lived at 6 Jixiang Lane, was sleeping in the room at noon when the fire broke out. He was unable to escape and died in the fire. He was 52 years old.

Old Society Dooms a Woman's Life 168

Six Clashes and Eight Defeats, Unable to Endure Abuse

Zhao Linzhen Resentfully Hangs Herself

Zhao Miaosheng, residing at No. 8 Cai Family Residence, Jiangwan Road, Zhabei, has a daughter named Linzhen, aged nineteen. Her nature is rather strong, but her mind is narrow. Zhao has a foster son, Tan Baobao, who is about the same age as Linzhen. They were childhood sweethearts, growing up together without suspicion. Therefore, the parents of both sides arranged a marriage for the young couple, making them an engaged couple. Unexpectedly, the Tan family's fortunes declined, and over several years, the grandfather and parents, among others, died one after another, leaving Tan alone. As a result, they were unable to marry for a time, and the villagers pointed out that Linzhen was cursed with "six clashes and eight defeats." Linzhen, under the control of this semi-civilized theocratic society, felt resentment and wanted to die. Therefore, she secretly bought opium and swallowed it to commit suicide, but was saved by her family. However, the pain in Linzhen's heart remained, so the night before last, she finally hanged herself. By the time her family found out and rescued her, it was too late. The beat police reported to the Fifth District Police Station, ordering Wang Jinfu, the local security officer of District 91, to report to the District Court for verification. Linzhen's father, Zhao Miaosheng, also petitioned the court for exemption from verification, which was approved by Prosecutor Yang Lu, who ordered him to sign a pledge to handle the funeral himself.

Chen Baixu's Funeral Today 169

Mr. Chen Baixu, a veteran member of the Jiangxi Min Party, engaged in revolutionary activities before 1911. He participated in every battle of the Wuchang Uprising, the Second and Third Revolutions, and the establishment of the Grand Marshal's Office in Guangzhou. He was a member of parliament and authored books such as "The National Revolution," "The Five-Power Constitution," and "Sun Yat-sen's Revolutionary Principles." However, due to poor health, he mostly recuperated at sea. He had been bedridden with lung disease since this spring for seven months. Although friends raised funds to treat him, he showed no improvement. He passed away at 3:05 PM on the 27th of this month. The funeral is scheduled for 2:00 PM today (the 29th). Chen's funeral arrangements are very simple; the coffin and clothing were provided by friends who pooled their money. They are now still trying to find ways to help his family make ends meet.

Housheng Employees Fight Over Bonus Case 170

Appealed to the Board of Directors' Meeting Minutes

Ruled to be Kept by Zhang Lanping

After the collapse of the Housheng Ziji Yarn Factory, the factory employees claimed that the accumulated bonuses over the years amounted to more than 900,000 taels, but had never been distributed in accordance with the regulations. Previously, Jiang Zhonghe, Zhou Qichang, Sun Kewei, Xu Dianhuang, and others were elected as representatives and retained lawyer Jiang Baoli to send a letter to manager Li Diguang, requesting that the bonuses be distributed in accordance with the regulations. Li refused, so they filed a petition with the First Special District Court to request custody of the factory's books so that the matter could be resolved according to law. The Special Court approved the request, and Judge He Jun led bailiffs and police officers to the factory's wholesale office in Yongqing Lane, Shandong Road, to verify the books and ledgers of previous years. He then ordered Wu Heqin, the chief accountant, to sign a pledge to keep them safe. However, it was discovered at the time that the minutes of the factory's board of directors had not been handed over by Wu. When questioned, he claimed that the minutes were kept by director Zhang Lanping. Judge He immediately ordered the original petitioners to file a petition to retrieve them. As a result, lawyer Jiang filed another petition, and Zhang Lanping was summoned yesterday afternoon. Zhang brought the minutes of the meeting with him and retained lawyer Chen Zhongyin to defend him. After Judge He examined the minutes, he found that they were quite important and immediately ordered Zhang Lanping to sign a pledge in court to be responsible for keeping them safe, pending further investigation.

Newly Discovered Parasitic Disease 173

A Conversation with Chen Fangzhi, Director of the Central Hygiene Testing Institute

Regarding the report recently published by various Chinese and Western newspapers in Shanghai about Dr. Jourdain, Director of the Public Concession Health Department, stating that a new type of parasitic disease has recently been discovered in Shanghai, which is very dangerous to those infected, an Echen Society reporter specially visited the Central Hygiene Testing Institute in Zhabei yesterday and interviewed Dr. Chen Fangzhi, the director of the institute. According to Dr. Chen, the year and month when this disease started are no longer known. There is no record of it in old medical books. Observing its widespread transmission, it is definitely not newly imported from foreign countries, nor is it a sudden disaster from the sky. It is just that people in the past were unaware of it. People in Jiaxing call this disease "𤵛 lump swelling," and people in Lin'an call it "loss of strength and yellowing." Academically, it can be translated as "blood leech disease." Hundreds of thousands of boatmen and farmers in the provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, and Hubei suffer from this disease. It is also quite prevalent near Shanghai and around Qingyang Port. According to my (the doctor refers to himself) investigation, the reason why this city is spared from this disease is mainly due to the rapid currents of the Huangpu River, which do not allow the intermediate host to settle. However, areas within thirty miles of the Huangpu River, such as Beixinjing, Zhenru, Zhengjiaqiao, and Puhuitang, and even farther away, such as Qingyang Port, are all plagued by it. Those who suffer from it are mostly farmers, boatmen, and slum dwellers, while those in the upper class who contract this disease through swimming or wading are rare. Dr. Chen also kindly presented the reporter with a special issue of the institute's "Research on Blood Leech Disease," which contains the results of the institute's research over the past three years. The reporter thanked him and then took his leave.

Continued Hearing on Rent Disputes in Shuntai Lane 180

According to tenants who have lived in Shuntai Lane for a long time, there are several shops on Baoshan Road outside the lane, which were completed gradually in 1919 and 1920. The rent has not been increased for many years. In February last year, the landlord proposed to increase the rent since 1924 due to the prosperity of the Zhabei market and the increase in land prices. However, after the tenants' representatives negotiated, the deadline was extended and an agreement was signed, stating that the rent would not be increased until 1931. Therefore, the notice issued by the landlord to increase the rent in 1932 is based on the previous agreement. It is said that the current rent for shikumen (stone-gate) houses in the lane is 19 yuan per month, and the rent for shops is 17 or 18 yuan. After the rent increase next year, the rent for three-story shikumen houses will be 24 yuan and change, and the rent for shops will be 30 yuan. The tenants in the lane have always had good relations with each other, and this dispute should be resolved soon.

Reader Correspondence

News from San Shi Jun in Nanchang 184

(Please Instruct the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association to Guide the Work of Resisting Japan in the Interior)

Since the incident of the Japanese invaders occupying the Eastern Provinces, all knowledgeable people have been loudly calling for "Resisting Japan and Saving the Nation" and "Economic Boycott." The media, in particular, have been working hard to promote this, hoping to awaken the people of the whole country and make them aware that national subjugation is imminent. Everyone should unite and save themselves and the country. I think that as long as people's hearts are not dead, this time there should be some effect. Shanghai is a place where business is concentrated, and the people are enlightened earlier. Since the organization of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, it has been working tirelessly and has already achieved considerable results. However, when you look at various cities in the interior, you see that the market is full of Japanese goods. Although there are also Anti-Japanese Associations, they are not doing the same thing. I am a young man oppressed by life. This time, I came to Nanchang to seek food and clothing. Nanchang is the capital of Jiangxi Province. All kinds of shops on the road hang Japanese goods in front of their doors to attract customers. Alas, it is still like this in the provincial capital. The situation in other counties can be imagined. After seeing the above situation, I was extremely distressed and thought of two methods. Please ask your newspaper to forward them to the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. If they can be done, I think they will be much better than the current methods. They are described as follows: (1) The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association should immediately select capable personnel to go to various provinces to contact the Anti-Japanese Associations in various provinces to carry out research on the most effective methods for each province (because the situation in each province is different). On the one hand, it will guide the Anti-Japanese Associations in various provinces to work hard. (2) The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association should print more shocking picture newspapers and post them in various provinces and cities. In addition, the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association should initiate a request for the Anti-Japanese Associations in various provinces to notify them of the progress of their work every three days for reference and to review whether they are working hard. Although the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association is organized by all sectors of Shanghai, I think that saving the country should not be limited by regional boundaries.

Special Coverage of Education News

Talking about Resisting Japan and Saving the Nation from the Standpoint of Education by Zhang Angqian 187

Since the Shenyang Incident, like a bolt from the blue, occurred, all patriotic people in our country have felt deep anger and resentment, hating to destroy the Japanese to avenge this great shame. However, there are many ways to save the country, and it cannot be achieved overnight. The efforts of ten years of recovery and ten years of education must rely on education.

Is it not clear that Japan's success today is entirely due to its vigorous emphasis on colonial education after the Meiji Restoration? Therefore, if we talk about saving the country today without making practical and effective preparations in terms of education, it is not a fundamental plan and will ultimately be of no help to the great cause of saving the country.

Now the alarm has sounded. The League of Nations has become a mere formality. At this critical juncture of survival, we can only focus on saving the country through education with this burning enthusiasm, in a calm and resolute manner. This long-term and sustained effort will not be difficult to fulfill. Otherwise, it will be dangerous. Now, please allow me to offer a few words to my colleagues in the education field who are engaged in basic work:

Regarding school administration, follow the outline of resisting Japan and saving the nation promulgated by the central government and educational administrative organs, refer to the school environment, determine the central activity plan for resisting Japan and saving the nation, formulate a calendar of events for resisting Japan and saving the nation, create charts, booklets, and reports of various processes for resisting Japan and saving the nation, and implement them effectively.

Regarding the school curriculum, formulate an outline of courses for resisting Japan and saving the nation in each subject, plan the allocation of courses for resisting Japan and saving the nation (for example, secondary schools and above can add or change to Japanese in the foreign language department to prepare for studying Japan), collect materials for resisting Japan and saving the nation in each subject, compile systematic teaching materials, and pay special attention to various sciences to enrich the content and improve the level to achieve real results.

Regarding teaching, determine the teaching syllabus for resisting Japan and saving the nation at all levels and in all subjects, select and read records and reports of Japan's invasion of China over the years and the recent forceful occupation of the three northeastern provinces, as well as the words, deeds, or biographies of our country's loyal and courageous patriots, practice studying Japanese anti-three northeastern provinces' texts and propaganda opinions and plans for resisting Japan and saving the nation, or hold regular contests for essays and speeches on resisting Japan and saving the nation, and formulate examination methods to assess students' achievements in resisting Japan and saving the nation.

Regarding training, follow the education outline of student volunteer army promulgated by the central government, organize volunteer armies, guide students to study Japan (with special emphasis on Japanese education, politics, economy, industry, military affairs, etc.) and participate in various anti-Japanese and national salvation activities, and engage in the investigation and statistics of Japanese goods (types, product names, manufacturing, sales, etc.) and domestic substitutes for Japanese goods. Elementary schools can also formulate slogans for resisting Japan and saving the nation (imitating training slogans) to be read aloud for a few minutes before class every day, and formulate songs for resisting Japan and saving the nation to be sung in unison at gatherings.

Regarding equipment, design and arrange various suitable environments for resisting Japan and saving the nation, and equip adequate important books, teaching aids, charts, and all propaganda pictures and slogans for resisting Japan and saving the nation to stimulate students' thoughts of resisting Japan and saving the nation and promote attention to the Japanese issue.

"If you want to have blessed oranges, you must go to China; if you want to have wide oranges, you must go to China." This is Japanese elementary education. "Investigate Manchurian products and study Chinese issues." This is Japanese secondary education and above. Ah, fellow countrymen, do you also know to rise up and not regard saving the country through education as a foolish talk? Encourage each other.

Important News

Newly Published Books Should Be Submitted for Review in Accordance with the Law 188

The Ministry of Education approved the document from the Hebei Provincial Government regarding the request to file the "Outline of Research Methods in Mathematics" compiled by Luo Gongquan, etc. The Ministry of Education found that it did not comply with the legal procedures and asked the provincial government to handle and reply to it in accordance with the regulations. The Ministry received a document from your government stating that it was based on a report from the Tianjin Municipal Government transferring the "Outline of Research Methods in Mathematics" compiled by Luo Gongquan to the Social Bureau for forwarding for filing, etc. The rest will be kept on file. In addition to preparing for inspection, two copies of the original attachments are enclosed for your reference and filing. The department's investigation found that all newly published books should be handled in accordance with the Publication Law promulgated by the National Government on December 16, 1930, and the regulations on submitting newly published books promulgated by the department on March 28, 1930. Those that are school textbooks must also comply with the review regulations for textbooks promulgated by the department on November 28, 1929. However, according to the author's original submission, the request is to review, register, and forward for filing, which seems to be based on the Copyright Law (see the National Government Gazette, No. 58) to apply for registration. However, the second article of the Copyright Law stipulates that the registration of copyright works is under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Internal Affairs. As for textbooks that should be reviewed by the department in accordance with the law, they will not be registered before being reviewed and approved by the department. In addition, the department previously received a request from the National Peiping Library to send the submitted newly published books to the Central Library. Before the Central Library was established, they were directly handed over to the library for storage, which has been approved and notified to all departments. The various clauses submitted by the Social Bureau are not legal and the procedures cannot be approved for filing. Accordingly, two copies of the original book are enclosed to reply for inspection and to instruct compliance with the above regulations separately.

Confirmation of Professor Laski's Visit to China 189

Regarding Professor Laski's visit to China, there were previous rumors that it had been called off. According to Mr. Kang Liwu, who is responsible for the contact, these rumors are completely untrue. Laski originally intended to depart at the end of October, but because he had just returned to the University of London from lecturing at Miami University at the end of September, the University of London firmly requested that he stay at the school to serve temporarily because Laski had been away from England for a year. Therefore, he recently sent a letter stating that the visit would be postponed until early January next year. As for the claim that the League of Nations changed its appointment of another professor to replace him because Laski was leftist, it is even more fabricated. Laski strongly criticized the impossibility of communism in other countries in his book "Communism." Moreover, the appointment of Laski was presided over by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee, which has nothing to do with the League of Nations. Furthermore, Mr. David, the exchange professor sent by the League of Nations, met with Mr. Kang yesterday and expressed his desire for Laski to come soon, which proves the absolute inaccuracy of the above rumors. In addition, the outline of Laski's thought, edited by Mr. Kang, is written by political scholars Xiao Gongquan, Lu Xirong, Wu Songgao, Shi Zhaoyun, and others, and is intended to introduce Laski's thought in advance. It is now being rushed to print by the Commercial Press.

Ministry of Education Promulgates Principles for Implementing the Three Principles of the People Education (7) 191

Section 2 Implementation Guidelines

1. Curriculum

1. The curriculum of all levels of schools should be based on the curriculum standards of schools at all levels in the interior and should be compiled in consideration of the situation in Mongolia and Tibet.

2. Textbooks for elementary schools should be compiled in Mongolian-Chinese and Tibetan-Chinese. Textbooks for secondary schools and above should be compiled in Chinese. In principle, the teaching materials for schools at all levels should pay special attention to the following points:

(1) The history of the integration of the Chinese nation; (2) The geographical relationship between the border regions and the interior; (3) The history and facts of imperialism's aggression against Mongolia and Tibet; (4) The relationship between the Mongolian and Tibetan people and the National Revolution; (5) The relationship between local autonomy of the Mongolian and Tibetan people and the Principle of Democracy; (6) The relationship between the economic undertakings of the Mongolian and Tibetan people and the Principle of People's Livelihood; (7) Other teaching materials related to the special environment of the Mongolian and Tibetan people.

2. Moral Education 192

1. Moral education at all levels of schools should be implemented based on the living conditions of the Mongolian and Tibetan people, with reference to the moral education standards of schools at all levels in the interior.

2. The implementation of moral education at all levels of schools should pay special attention to the following points: (1) Use scientific common sense to break their superstitions about the natural world; (2) Awaken national spirit to break their tribal thinking.

3. Cultivate the spirit of loving the country and the nation through the explanation of international current affairs and the training of group life.

3. Equipment 193

1. The equipment of all levels of schools should be based on the spirit of the Three Principles of the People and the special environment of Mongolia and Tibet.

2. The equipment of all levels of schools should pay special attention to the following points: (3) Prepare more books and charts related to Mongolia and Tibet; (2) Display more cultural relics from the interior.

The Results of the Petition Are Considered Satisfactory

The military training department of the Anti-Japanese Associations of various universities in the city, which previously sent representatives Hu Wenquan and Wen Guangyi to Nanjing on the evening of the 25th to petition the Training Supervision Department and the Central Party Headquarters for the rapid allocation of firearms and instructors for inspection, etc., returned to Shanghai at 8:00 AM yesterday. It is said that the results of the petition were satisfactory. Firearms and instructors will be distributed within a week. A concrete plan for military education is also being drafted and will be issued soon. The program will last approximately six months, with a minimum of two hours of training per day. The titles are divided into three categories: (A) Youth Volunteer Army for junior high school students and above; (B) Volunteer Army for junior high school students and below; (C) People's Volunteer Army organized by community groups, etc.

Shanghai Branch of the Anti-Japanese Association of Students Studying in Japan Yesterday Petitioned to Stop Japan's Enticement of Students Studying in Japan 195

Using Selection Fees to Entice Students to Prevent Them from Returning Home

A Strong Protest Should Be Lodged with the Japanese Cultural Affairs Department

Since its establishment, the Shanghai branch of the All China Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of Students Studying in Japan has been actively engaged in its work. The association recently received a report from students in Tokyo stating that the Japanese are misusing the Boxer Indemnity selection fee (originally intended to provide scholarships to outstanding students) to entice students studying in Japan to prevent them from returning home and engaging in active anti-Japanese activities. The association believes that this matter concerns the loss of national prestige and the disruption of the overall situation. Yesterday, it sent a letter to the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Municipal Education Bureau, and the Nanjing General Association of the association, requesting them to forward it to Jiang Zuobin, the Chinese ambassador to Japan, and Liu Suichang, the supervisor of students studying abroad, to strictly prohibit this practice and to urge them to quickly lodge a strong protest with the Japanese Cultural Affairs Department, preventing them from misusing selection fee quotas to anesthetize Chinese students in Japan and prevent them from returning home to participate in the anti-Japanese movement. The association has also been designated by the Municipal Party Headquarters to move to the First District Party Headquarters in Meijia Lane in the South City and will hold a general meeting of all members on the first day of next month to elect officers and discuss important issues.

(5) The number of members of the presidium should be determined. Resolved: 15 members will be appointed, with one chairman elected by the presidium. (6) How should the commander-in-chief be determined? Resolved: The commander-in-chief will be appointed by the presidium. (7) How should the proposals for the conference be handled? Resolved: The conference documentation department will solicit proposals from various schools. (8) The date of the next meeting should be determined. Resolved: October 30th at 10:00 AM.

Creating a Middle School Reading Sports Meet Amidst the National Crisis 202

The Middle School Preparatory Committee for the National Crisis Reading Sports Meet held a conference in the school's auditorium on Fuxu Road on the 26th of this month. A summary is provided below:

Gao Naitong's speech: Mr. Gao is the director of research at the school. At the opening, he briefly stated that the school is holding a reading sports meet amidst the national crisis for two purposes: (1) to awaken the people to prepare strength and focus on fundamental solutions; (2) to contribute to reading methods. He also stated that the school is not trying to be unconventional by advocating the high tone of reading sports amidst the calls for boycotting classes to save the nation. The reason is that education in our country is not widespread and there are too few readers, so saving the nation must start with readers. Next, he introduced the honorary chairman of the association.

Pan Yangyao gave a speech titled "How to Read During the National Crisis," briefly stating that in the face of the national crisis, educators should first blame themselves. As Mr. Gao said, we should prepare strength and focus on fundamental solutions. Young students saving the nation through reading is the current urgent task, and we should read science books and address the current urgent questions. The only method for reading is "sincerity," hoping that everyone will strive for it. The audience applauded. Next, Yang Weiyu was invited to give a speech titled "Reading and Saving the Nation," quoting the remarks made by Mr. Hu Hanmin, briefly stating that the present is a world of science, not just a struggle of military force, but a competition of the entire country, and strongly criticized the Chinese people for not studying the Northeast issue and instructing the youth on the direction of reading and saving the nation. His words were poignant and moved the audience. Then,

Du Dingyou gave a speech in which Mr. Du reported on his reading experience, detailing the poverty of his family environment, the confused life in elementary school, the disorganized life in middle school, and the diligent life while studying abroad. He has been reading constantly for more than ten years, repeatedly citing evidence, and his words were full of warnings, keeping the audience from tiring. Then,

Ye Xin'an gave a speech. Mr. Ye's speech had two topics: (1) Reading Methods; (2) Dictionary Problems. He reported on his own reading experience, supplemented by scientific methods, and reported on the process of inventing the four-corner coding method and his determination to reform the dictionary. It was fluent and eloquent, lasting for an hour, and the audience applauded. Finally,

Gao Naitong gave a thank-you speech, saying that the reading movement is still in its infancy in our country, and hoping that the people of the country will strive together after this movement to achieve results. The meeting ended as the bell rang seven times.

Free Talk

The Voice of Resistance

— Zhiqiang

Amidst the passionate voices of resistance, it is unfortunate that a very disheartening incident has occurred in our telecommunications sector. The content of this incident is that the Shanghai International Radio Station has been secretly colluding with Japan. The main culprits are the station's reporting director, Wei Daming, and two others. The Ministry of Transportation has been informed of this and will dismiss Wei and the other two and investigate them. This is not a trivial matter. We must ensure that this kind of thing does not happen again in the future. I sincerely hope that everyone, in such a tense atmosphere, will use their clear minds to think for themselves, their families, society, and the nation. Do not be tempted or seduced by any force. Do not let them blacken your conscience for nothing. I do not know what Wei and the others were thinking. I do not know what severe punishment the authorities will give them. I can only encourage myself and my compatriots across the country not to follow in their footsteps.

Chat Collection of the No Grass in the Courtyard Studio

Better to Learn from Al (Below) 208

Al's mother is truly invaluable, allowing him to keep those poisons at home, as many as two hundred bottles! The conductor on the train is also interesting, actually letting him set up a laboratory on the baggage car! These are all angels who care for science and children. If there were no such angels, then where could Al, who is not tolerated in formal schools, be tolerated in the family and society? Children should not give up on themselves. Are there no places to study hard other than schools? Look at Al, he is tired of the dead education of schools, so he goes home and does experiments at home, and does experiments on the train. If he doesn't have money, he sells newspapers and vegetables, and uses the money he earns to do experiments. He lives a scientific life and receives a scientific education. Isn't this true life education? He and his little partners do it themselves, learn it themselves, and teach it themselves. Isn't this evidence of the integration of teaching, learning, and doing? The New York Times said that the capital invested in Edison's (Al's grown-up form) inventions and the businesses driven by his inventions totals $150 million, equivalent to $700 million in Chinese currency. Everyone says that China is pitifully poor. The only way to alleviate poverty is to create a wealthy society, not just wealthy individuals. The United States used Edison to create many rich people, but we want to use the future Edison to create a rich country for 400 million people and a rich world for 2 billion people. How will this future Edison come about? When he is young, he is Al, and when he grows up, he naturally becomes Edison. As long as the teachers scold the bad eggs a little less, and society, the family, and the government give a little more freedom and use a little less uniformity, Al, the Edison, will emerge like bamboo shoots after rain and be unstoppable.

A Glimpse of the Recent Situation in Japan 209

— Yiweishi

A certain Western newspaper reporter recently came to Shanghai from Japan. According to him, since the invasion of the Eastern Provinces, the situation in that country has become very tense. There are indeed many Japanese citizens who are dissatisfied with the military's dictatorial and aggressive policies. However, the government is controlled and manipulated by the military, and it severely suppresses public opinion that opposes the military's policies. On the one hand, it prohibits newspapers from publishing opinions against the use of force. On the other hand, it fabricates rumors of Chinese bandits infringing on the lives and property of Japanese people in order to incite its people to unite against us. All news and information published in newspapers are inspected by the censorship bureau. News about military actions is not allowed to be published unless it is distributed by their official sources. Therefore, the Japanese people know nothing about the truth of the Japanese military's brutality and cruelty in China. Japanese domestic thought is very complex. There are quite a few believers in socialism and communism. This is especially true for Japanese people who have received higher education, such as university students. The authorities are very vigilant against these elements, fearing that they will explode and be detrimental to the invasion of China. On the one hand, they are closely monitored by police detectives. On the other hand, they promote sports in order to consume their energy and thoughts and divert the attention of domestic youth. Therefore, baseball competitions are held almost every day. Even in the rain, they do not stop. The authorities are always worried about the thoughts of university students, so they conduct a test of opinions on China. The questions were "Is Manchuria related to the lifeblood of Japan?" and "Is Japan's action in Manchuria justified this time?" The results showed that 90% of the respondents gave affirmative answers to both questions. Thus, the authorities began to feel a little relieved. The reason why the majority of the university students answered in this way is that the Japanese authorities fabricate facts and declare internally.

Brothers have been planning peace for a long time, but it has not been achieved. I am shocked to hear that the strong enemy has already approached the city. On the Ninth Day of the Lunar Year Xinwei, Brother Feng Zhenxin Showed Me the Landscape Painting "Blue Water Flows from a Thousand Valleys, Jade Mountain is Tall with Two Peaks Cold" by His Teacher, Mr. Xia Jiancheng, and Asked Me to Write a Poem. Each young man speaks of joining the army.

Confucians who cool their blood with rot deserve to be killed.

Amid national crisis, annotating "Shuowen Jiezi."

This is the power of propaganda. Several weeks ago, there were still many in Japan who opposed using force against China. Record of a Flower Plunder Marked by Teeth 214

— Jing Mengdie

In the southwest of Wujin County, there is a small village called Putang, inhabited by only six or seven families. Among them, the head of the Li family lost his sight early in life and made a living by fortune-telling, commonly known as "Blind Li." His livelihood was not bad, with annual surpluses. Furthermore, being blind, his food and clothing expenses were frugal, so he accumulated some wealth and became well-off. The villagers all called Blind Li a rich man. Blind Li had no son, only one daughter, of marriageable age. He intended to find a son-in-law to live with them and support him in his old age, but he had not yet found a suitable one.

Recently, bandits have been rampant, and robbery has become a common practice. Many idle young men in the village have banded together to become thieves, thinking that Blind Li has a lot of money and that he would be easy to deal with. One night last month, a group of seven or eight thieves came and broke into his house. Blind Li, as if following the Liaoning people's non-resistance policy against the Japanese pirates, allowed them to rummage through boxes and cabinets, sweeping away everything. Fortunately, Blind Li had most of his remaining wealth loaned out, so the loss was not too great. The thieves, not satisfied with what they had taken, saw that Li's daughter was beautiful. So they tied her hands and feet and took turns raping her. The delicate flower and tender bud were brutally ravaged. The girl's resentment and anger can be imagined. By the sixth person, after satisfying his bestial desires, he lowered his head and leaned in, wanting to kiss her. Unexpectedly, the girl used all her strength to bite his shoulder fiercely, as if venting the resentment she felt from the six men on one person. The thief, in pain, got up. It was almost dawn. He let out a shout, and they scattered like birds and beasts.

After the thieves left, the girl was bedridden for several days before she got up. Because it was far from the city, she had not reported it to the authorities. The thieves thought, "What can Blind Li do?" and went unpunished. Several miles east of the village, there is a town called Xinan, which is a market town. One afternoon, the girl walked to the market to buy things. At the end of the street, she caught a glimpse of a man who looked exactly like the sixth thief who had plundered the flower that night. The thief, suddenly encountering the girl, hesitated and wanted to avoid her. The girl immediately smiled sweetly at him. The thief smiled back, secretly pleased that the girl still recognized him and had not forgotten him. He thought that the bite he received that night was not out of hatred but out of love, almost like the ancient "biting the arm to make an alliance." So he slowly followed the girl, gradually starting a conversation. He asked her to go to a certain hotel west of the town. The girl gladly agreed, telling him to go in first and saying that she had some small matters to attend to and might not return that night. The thief was overjoyed and entered a room in the hotel, waiting for the beauty, thinking it would be a real delight, far better than the hasty act of the previous time. Before long, the girl led several policemen to the hotel. The thief realized he had been tricked, but there was no escape, so he surrendered. The thief was from the town. After he was taken to the police station, his friends, Mr. A and Mr. B, came one after another, wanting to vouch for him, saying that this person was not a thief but just a lecher, perhaps. The girl resolutely stated the facts in public, and said that the bite mark on his shoulder would not disappear in a short time, the mark was still recognizable. Why not take off his clothes and check? The police chief ordered him to strip and looked at it, and the tooth marks were clearly visible, with scabs still on the wound. He confessed after one interrogation. He was transferred to the court for sentencing. People admired the girl's quick wit and laughed at the thief for not dying for money but for dying for lust. The magic power of beauty is even greater than gold, they said.

Chronology of Japanese Aggression Against China and Various Massacres (V) 215

— Zhi

1923 (Republic of China Year 12) (1) Japan returned Qingdao to us with extremely harsh conditions. At the same time, it allowed us to redeem the Jiaoji Railway for 40 million yuan. (2) In the same year, the lease term for Lushun and Dalian expired. Japan refused to return them. (3) In February, a Japanese employee of a Japanese trading firm in Hankou falsely accused a Chinese worker, Tian Zhongxiang, of stealing a watch and beat him to death. (4) On June 1, the Japanese army massacred patriotic Chinese students and the masses in Changsha, Hunan. (5) In September, a major earthquake occurred in Tokyo, Yokohama, and other places in Japan. Order was disrupted. The Japanese army took the opportunity to massacre hundreds of overseas Chinese, students, and workers.

1924 (Republic of China Year 13) (1) Japan decided to return the Boxer Indemnity, but used it for cultural undertakings in China. It set up a special bureau under Japanese control to carry out cultural aggression. (2) In January, dozens of Japanese Taiwanese people in Xiamen, Fujian, looted and caused disturbances. The Japanese government protected the Taiwanese bandits and sent warships to Xiamen, threatening our country not to suppress the bandits. (3) In February, a Japanese merchant in Hankou, Ubatada Zo, strangled a Chinese man, Mai Bangmin.

1925 (Republic of China Year 14) (1) On May 15, a Japanese cotton mill murdered Gu Zhenghong, a Chinese worker. This led to the May 30th massacre on Nanjing Road in Shanghai. (2) In October, the Beijing government convened a tariff conference. The Japanese representative's proposal secretly aimed to delay China's tariff autonomy. (3) In December, Guo Songling rebelled against Fengtian. Japan sent troops to Manchuria to help Zhang Zuolin kill Guo Songling.

1926 (Republic of China Year 15) In March, Japan, under the pretext of protecting its nationals, sent warships to Tianjin to help the Fengtian army attack the National Revolutionary Army. It shelled the Dagu Forts and used machine guns to mow down our defending soldiers. Later, it even lobbied the diplomatic corps in Beijing to jointly pressure our country. Beijing students petitioned the Duan government, leading to the March 18th massacre.

1927 (Republic of China Year 16) (1) On March 24, warships from Britain, the United States, Italy, France, and other countries shelled our revolutionary army and civilians in Nanjing, causing many casualties. (2) In April, Japanese sailors shot and killed a Chinese rickshaw puller in Hankou. When the civilians argued with them, they used machine guns to mow down more than a dozen people and injured dozens more. (3) In May, Japan, under the pretext of protecting its nationals, sent more than 2,000 troops directly into Shandong, hindering the advance of our revolutionary army. (4) On June 27, Tanaka convened the Eastern Conference to plan an active policy of aggression against Manchuria and Mongolia. (5) In July, Japan sent troops to Shandong for the second time. (6) In early August, the Dalian Conference discussed how to implement the resolutions of the Eastern Conference regarding the active policy towards Manchuria and Mongolia. It was later moved to Lushun. At the same time, Japanese soldiers in Benxihu massacred Chinese workers again.

Special Features of "Second Visit to the Palace" 216

— Shaoqing

"Second Visit to the Palace" is the most beautiful to listen to in opera. It has the following four characteristics: 1. Triangular singing, either a line or a section, with alternating and intricate arrangements, creating changes in the singing style. 2. Consecutive singing of "erhuang kuai yuanban," with no interlude left after the top beat, like rapid questions and answers, extremely tight. 3. Adding filler words to form long sentences, causing changes in the rhythm. 4. The play has only one scene with three different voices. Three different roles stand side by side, without distinction between guest and host, like a three-color bookplate or a three-color porcelain, with extremely rich colors. Therefore, this play cannot be performed without three good actors with good voices and seniority singing together. Because it is not easy to find suitable partners, it is not often performed on stage. Yesterday, at a friend's house, I happened to hear a new Gaoting record of Shang Xiaoyun and Wang Shaolou singing "Second Visit to the Palace." It was truly a perfect match. This record starts from the big painted face singing "Holding the young emperor, I grasp the country," and continues with "yuanban" and "yaoban" until the end of the play at "Protecting the country is still up to you, the Yang family, father and son." It contains four sections in total. Shang Xiaoyun's voice is excellent, singing the typical role of a chaste and virtuous woman. There are many striking phrases, such as "You say he has no intention of usurpation," using the "jie jie gao" high pitch, resounding through the clouds, smooth and natural. "The empress dowager kneels to death in Zhaoyang," with a pause on the word "death," and the three words "in Zhaoyang" inflected appropriately, comparable to Chen Delin. The sentence "May your sons and grandsons have high rank and wealth" is completely flipped to a high pitch, effortless. Wang Shaolou sings in the style of Tan, with an excellent voice, singing in harmony with the music. For example, "Frightening the minister to lower his head and dare not look up" is sung with an emphasis on the tune, like a towering peak. The sentence "Accompanying the emperor before the mountain, they also captured Li Gang" requires a delicate vocal technique in a very fast tempo. The rest is all smooth and lively. Qiu Guixian is the only copper hammer big painted face, like a grand bell, majestic and generous, with absolutely no vulgarity. Singing the word "mai" in "The old minister is old" fills the cavity and fills with sound, like an old tree blooming. The two sentences "Li Wen died with an arrow at the north gate" and "When you think about it in the end" have a particularly rich flavor. The fast "yuanban" of more than twenty sentences sung by the three flows like clouds and flowing water, completed in one breath. Only with the equal strength of the three can this be achieved.

Rotary Club Novel

The Pestle of Knocking on Dreams (27) 217

— Cheng Zhanlu

"Layman, no need to say more; this gentle pestle cannot be considered a tool to awaken the national soul! Pay attention! There are ten, a hundred, a thousand, ten thousand times more pestles for knocking on dreams than this old monk has, to shatter your infatuated dreams! Your reliant dreams! Your dreams of being intoxicated with material civilization and lavishly consuming imported goods! Your dreams of blindly believing in military unification and only focusing inward! And other, other dreams that create future slaves and beasts! Layman, this pestle of knocking on dreams, weighing a thousand pounds, ten thousand pounds, will strike you head-on! You must be careful!"

Tao Chi exclaimed "Oh dear!" as if struck by a thunderbolt from the blue, receiving a major blow. When he opened his eyes, there was no elder, no revolving chair, no Unobstructed Hermitage, no horse tied to the large locust tree; everything was a dream.

Not only was his roaming in the modern paradise a dream, but also his journey into the past world was a dream. Both times he sat on the revolving chair were dreams. Tying the horse to the large locust tree and entering the Unobstructed Hermitage was a dream; riding the horse and running in all directions, unable to pass, was also a dream. The elder's pestle of knocking on dreams only woke him from a dream within a dream; though he was awake, he was still dreaming! Only this blow from the pestle of knocking on dreams truly awakened Tao Chi.

Who was the person knocking on dreams? It was Tao Chi's mother. What material was the pestle of knocking on dreams made of? It was a roll of that day's newspaper. It turned out that Tao Chi was feeling depressed because of the country's difficult situation. "When you're bored, you tend to doze off," and he had fallen asleep in the automatic chair! His mother, holding a roll of that day's newspaper, tapped him on the head, and he received a major blow, like a thunderbolt striking him head-on!

He opened the newspaper and saw the prominent headlines:

"Brutal Japan Occupies Shenyang! Mass Burning and Killing!"

"Brutal Japan Occupies Jilin! Extremely Tragic Massacre!"

"Northeast Airfield Seized by Brutal Japan! More Than Two Hundred Aircraft All Had National Emblems Painted Over!"

"The Large-Scale Shenyang Arsenal Looted by Brutal Japan!"

"The League of Nations Advises Brutal Japan, But Is Rejected!"

"Brutal Japan Falsely Claims Withdrawal, Treating the League of Nations Like a Child's Game!"

"League of Nations Adjourns!"

"Brutal Japan Issues Serious Warning to the National Government Regarding Our Patriotic Movement!"

"················!"

"················!" (The End)

It generates heat freely anytime, anywhere. It costs only two cents per hour to use. The style is clever and easy to use. It is truly an unprecedented invention and has been approved for a patent by the National Government. It has begun to be issued, and the price is low. Samples and instructions are available, and will be mailed upon request. Dasheng Gramophone Company declares that our company has always been famous in the Shanghai record industry for its large scale and perfect products. After the original building at No. 221 Nanjing Road was renovated, it moved to No. 360 Nanjing Road (west end of Pentang Lane). The new site is more luxuriously decorated, and the seating in the test room is comfortable. High-quality original gramophones are used to test the sound, so that customers can choose and decide what to take. All new automatic electric motors, famous singer records, movie song records, etc. are complete. The grand opening sale has been held since the previous day.

Huaxing Company declares that the German Hengpei Chemical Plant's cough medicine tablets, managed by our company, are effective remedies specifically for colds, coughs, pulmonary tuberculosis, and chronic respiratory diseases. Yong'an, Sincere, Zhongfa, Dalu Pharmacies, etc. in this city all sell them, and sales are very good.
